+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}, {@link sep.tinee.server} and
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}. Finally, you submit only your client code, which
+ * will be tested against the base framework as provided.
+ *
+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.
+ */
+package sep.mvc;
+
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.util.logging.Level;
+import java.util.logging.Logger;
+
+/**
+ * A View provides the front-end user interface, which includes appropriate
+ * presentation of the relevant model data to the user. The lifetime of an MVC
+ * application is often tied to its front-end UI.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * The View accepts user input, and conveys the corresponding commands to the
+ * registered {@linkplain sep.mvc.AbstractController Controller} for
+ * processing. The View interacts closely with the Controller, but should not
+ * be coupled to any particular Controller (i.e., a View should be
+ * interoperable with different Controllers).
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * A View may itself determine when it should be updated, and retrieve the
+ * required information directly from the
+ * {@linkplain sep.mvc.AbstractModel Model}, or operations performed on the
+ * Model (as directed by the Controller) may actively push updates to the View,
+ * or some combination thereof. The design can depend on whether the UI
+ * supports synchronous or asynchronous user interactions.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public abstract class AbstractView {
+
+  private AbstractController control;
+
+  /**
+   * This View is created without a registered Controller. A Controller is
+   * registered by passing this View when the Controller is created.
+   *
+   * @see #setController(sep.mvc.AbstractController)
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L51">  protected AbstractView() {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L52">    this.control = null;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L53">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Initialise this View. To be called once, and only once, before
+   * {@link #run()}.  It checks that this View has been registered with a
+   * {@linkplain sep.mvc.AbstractController Controller} (by supplying it as an
+   * argument to the Controller constructor call).
+   * &lt;p&gt;
+   * May be called by the top-level application bootstrapper (e.g., the
+   * {@code main} method).
+   *
+   * @throws IllegalStateException If no Controller has been registered.
+   */
+  public void init() {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L67" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.control == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L68">      throw new IllegalStateException(&quot;[MVC error] &quot;</span>
+          + &quot;This View has not been passed to a Controller.&quot;);
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L71">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Close this View. This operation is idempotent.
+   */
+  public abstract void close();
+
+  /* UI */
+
+  /**
+   * Start the overall MVC application after it has been assembled -- starts
+   * the main UI loop. Maintains an up-to-date presentation of the front-end
+   * user interface (e.g., via {@link #update()}), and interprets user
+   * input as commands for the Controller to process.
+   * &lt;p&gt;
+   * Should be called by the top-level application bootstrapper (e.g.,
+   * the {@code main} method) &lt;i&gt;after&lt;/i&gt; {@code init} has been called.
+   * &lt;p&gt;
+   * Precondition: {@link #init()} has been called.
+   *
+   * @throws IOException If a user input error occurs
+   */
+  public abstract void run() throws IOException;
+
+  /**
+   * Update the presentation of the front-end UI. May be called by
+   * {@link #run()}, or from the model/Controller, as appropriate for the
+   * application and UI design.
+   */
+  public abstract void update();
+
+  /* Getters */
+
+  /**
+   * Get the Controller registered to this View, if any.
+   *
+   * @return The registered Controller, if any
+   * @throws IllegalStateException If no Controller has been registered
+   */
+  protected AbstractController getController() {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L111" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.control == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L112">      throw new IllegalStateException(&quot;[MVC error] &quot;</span>
+          + &quot;This View has not been bound to a Controller.&quot;);
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L115">    return this.control;</span>
+  }
+
+  /**
+   * Get the model bound to the registered Controller, if a Controller has been
+   * registered.
+   *
+   * @return The bound model, if a Controller has been registered
+   * @throws IllegalStateException If no Controller has been registered
+   */
+  protected AbstractModel getModel() {
+<span class="nc" id="L126">    return getController().getModel();  // Checks if a Controller registered</span>
+  }
+
+  /* Auxiliary */
+
+  /**
+   * Registers the Controller if one has not been registered so far; otherwise
+   * the supplied Controller is shut down. Implicitly called by the
+   * {@link sep.mvc.AbstractController#AbstractController(AbstractModel, AbstractView)}
+   * constructor. Normally, you should not need to override this method.
+   *
+   * @param control The Controller to register
+   * @throws IllegalArgumentException If registering a null Controller
+   */
+  protected void setController(final AbstractController control) {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L141" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (control == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L142">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;[MVC error] Registering a null Controller.&quot;);
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L145" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.control != null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L146">      Logger.getLogger(AbstractView.class.getName()).log(Level.SEVERE,</span>
+          &quot;[MVC error] Controller already set.  Shutting down.&quot;);
+<span class="nc" id="L148">      control.shutdown();</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L150">    this.control = control;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L151">  }</span>
+}

+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Strict//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-strict.dtd"><html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" lang="en"><head><meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html;charset=UTF-8"/><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/report.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="shortcut icon" href="../.resources/report.gif" type="image/gif"/><title>ClientChannel.java</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/prettify.css" type="text/css"/><script type="text/javascript" src="../.resources/prettify.js"></script></head><body onload="window['PR_TAB_WIDTH']=4;prettyPrint()"><div class="breadcrumb" id="breadcrumb"><span class="info"><a href="../.sessions.html" class="el_session">Sessions</a></span><a href="../index.html" class="el_report">JaCoCoverage analysis of project &quot;18001953&quot; (powered by JaCoCo from EclEmma)</a> &gt; <a href="index.source.html" class="el_package">sep.tinee.net.channel</a> &gt; <span class="el_source">ClientChannel.java</span></div><h1>ClientChannel.java</h1><pre class="source lang-java linenums">/*
+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}, {@link sep.tinee.server} and
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}. Finally, you submit only your client code, which
+ * will be tested against the base framework as provided.
+ *
+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.
+ */
+package sep.tinee.net.channel;
+
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.io.ObjectInputStream;
+import java.io.ObjectOutputStream;
+import java.net.Socket;
+import java.util.logging.Level;
+import java.util.logging.Logger;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.Message;
+
+/**
+ * A client-side channel for interacting with an instance of
+ * {@code sep.tinee.server.Server}.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Usage protocol:
+ * &lt;ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt;
+ * Create a new instance of
+ * {@linkplain #ClientChannel(String, int) ClientChannel} supplying the host
+ * name and port number of the server.
+ * &lt;li&gt;
+ * Use {@linkplain #send(Message) send} and {@linkplain #receive() receive} to
+ * exchange instances of {@link sep.tinee.net.message.Message} with the
+ * server. These calls may be performed in any &lt;i&gt;sequence&lt;/i&gt; (note:
+ * {@code ClientChannel} is &lt;i&gt;not&lt;/i&gt; thread-safe) that respects the message
+ * protocol (see the documentation for each message), and any number of times
+ * (possibly zero), up to the occurrence of any error (&lt;i&gt;e.g.&lt;/i&gt;,
+ * {@code IOException}).
+ * &lt;li&gt;
+ * Use {@linkplain #close() close} to close the communication session.
+ * &lt;/ul&gt;
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public class ClientChannel implements AutoCloseable {
+
+  private final String host;
+  private final int port;
+
+  private Socket sock;  // isOpen() &lt;=&gt; this.sock != null
+  private ObjectOutputStream out;
+  private ObjectInputStream in;
+
+  /**
+   * Allocate a new client channel object for communicating with an instance of
+   * {@code sep.tinee.server.Server} listening at the specified host and port.
+   *
+   * @param host The server host, &lt;i&gt;e.g.&lt;/i&gt;, {@code &quot;localhost&quot;}
+   * @param port The server port, &lt;i&gt;e.g.&lt;/i&gt;, {@code 8888}
+   */
+<span class="fc" id="L65">  public ClientChannel(final String host, final int port) {</span>
+<span class="fc" id="L66">    this.host = host;</span>
+<span class="fc" id="L67">    this.port = port;</span>
+<span class="fc" id="L68">    this.sock = null;</span>
+<span class="fc" id="L69">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Returns {@code true} if, and only if, this channel is open, meaning that
+   * it currently encapsulates a TCP socket.
+   *
+   * @return whether this channel is currently open
+   */
+  public boolean isOpen() {
+<span class="pc bpc" id="L78" title="1 of 2 branches missed.">    return sock != null;</span>
+  }
+
+  private void open() throws IOException {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L82" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (!isOpen()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L83">      this.sock = new Socket(host, port);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L84">      this.out = new ObjectOutputStream(this.sock.getOutputStream());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L85">      this.in = new ObjectInputStream(this.sock.getInputStream());</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L87">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Send a message to the server specified at channel creation.
+   *
+   * @param msg The message to send
+   * @throws IOException If an I/O error occurs
+   */
+  public void send(final Message msg) throws IOException {
+    try {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L97" title="All 2 branches missed.">      if (isOpen()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L98">        this.out.reset();</span>
+      } else {
+<span class="nc" id="L100">        open();</span>
+      }
+<span class="nc" id="L102">      this.out.writeObject(msg);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L103">      this.out.flush();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L104">    } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L106">        close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L107">      } catch (IOException ex1) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L108">        Logger.getLogger(ClientChannel.class.getName()).log(Level.WARNING,</span>
+            &quot;Connection close error: &quot;, ex1);
+<span class="nc" id="L110">      }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L111">      throw ex;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L112">    }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L113">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Receive a message from the server specified at channel creation. This
+   * method blocks (&lt;i&gt;i.e.&lt;/i&gt;, does not return) until a message is received,
+   * or an error occurs.
+   *
+   * @return The received message, if successful
+   * @throws IOException            If an I/O error occurs
+   * @throws ClassNotFoundException Class of serialized object cannot be found
+   */
+  public Message receive() throws IOException, ClassNotFoundException {
+    Object obj;
+    try {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L127" title="All 2 branches missed.">      if (!isOpen()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L128">        open();</span>
+      }
+<span class="nc" id="L130">      obj = this.in.readObject();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L131">    } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L133">        close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L134">      } catch (IOException ex1) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L135">        Logger.getLogger(ClientChannel.class.getName()).log(Level.WARNING,</span>
+            &quot;Connection close error: &quot;, ex1);
+<span class="nc" id="L137">      }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L138">      throw ex;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L139">    }</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L140" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (!(obj instanceof Message)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L141">      throw new IOException(&quot;[Server error]  Received unexpected object type: &quot;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L142">          + obj.getClass());</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L144">    return (Message) obj;</span>
+  }
+
+  /**
+   * Close the encapsulated socket and I/O streams, if any currently open.
+   * &lt;p&gt;
+   * Guaranteed post condition: {@code !isOpen()}. This operation is idempotent
+   * provided the other methods are not called.
+   *
+   * @throws IOException If an I/O error occurs
+   */
+  @Override
+  public void close() throws IOException {
+<span class="nc" id="L157">    IOException err = null;</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L158" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.in != null) {</span>
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L160">        this.in.close();  // Idempotent</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L161">      } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L162">        err = ex;  // err currently null</span>
+      } finally {
+<span class="nc" id="L164">        this.in = null;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L165">      }</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L167" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.out != null) {</span>
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L169">        this.out.close();  // Idempotent</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L170">      } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L171" title="All 2 branches missed.">        if (err == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L172">          err = ex;</span>
+        }
+      } finally {
+<span class="nc" id="L175">        this.out = null;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L176">      }</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L178" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.sock != null) {  // i.e., isOpen</span>
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L180">        this.sock.close();  // Idempotent</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L181">      } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L182" title="All 2 branches missed.">        if (err == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L183">          err = ex;</span>
+        }
+      } finally {
+<span class="nc" id="L186">        this.sock = null;  // isOpen -&gt; false</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L187">      }</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L189" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (err != null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L190">      throw err;</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L192">  }</span>
+}

+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},

+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.

+package sep.tinee.net.message;
+
+/**
+ * A {@code BYE} message: Tell a {@link sep.tinee.server.Server} instance to
+ * terminate this communication session. No further messages should be sent or
+ * received in this session.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Instances of this class are immutable.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public class Bye implements Message {
+
+  private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;  // Default
+
+  /**
+   * The header code.
+   */
+  public static final String HEADER = &quot;BYE&quot;;
+
+  /**
+   * Create a {@code BYE} message.
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L38">  public Bye() {</span>
+    // Empty constructor
+<span class="nc" id="L40">  }</span>
+
+  @Override
+  public String getHeader() {
+<span class="nc" id="L44">    return Bye.HEADER;</span>
+  }
+
+  @Override
+  public String toString() {
+<span class="nc" id="L49">    return Bye.HEADER;</span>
+  }
+}

+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Strict//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-strict.dtd"><html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" lang="en"><head><meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html;charset=UTF-8"/><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/report.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="shortcut icon" href="../.resources/report.gif" type="image/gif"/><title>Message.java</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/prettify.css" type="text/css"/><script type="text/javascript" src="../.resources/prettify.js"></script></head><body onload="window['PR_TAB_WIDTH']=4;prettyPrint()"><div class="breadcrumb" id="breadcrumb"><span class="info"><a href="../.sessions.html" class="el_session">Sessions</a></span><a href="../index.html" class="el_report">JaCoCoverage analysis of project &quot;18001953&quot; (powered by JaCoCo from EclEmma)</a> &gt; <a href="index.source.html" class="el_package">sep.tinee.net.message</a> &gt; <span class="el_source">Message.java</span></div><h1>Message.java</h1><pre class="source lang-java linenums">/*
+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}, {@link sep.tinee.server} and
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}. Finally, you submit only your client code, which
+ * will be tested against the base framework as provided.
+ *
+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.
+ */
+package sep.tinee.net.message;
+
+import java.io.Serializable;
+
+/**
+ * A base interface for messages that can be communicated using
+ * {@link sep.tinee.net.channel.ClientChannel} with an instance of
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server.Server}.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public interface Message extends Serializable {
+
+  /**
+   * Returns the &lt;i&gt;unique&lt;/i&gt; header code for this message. The code should be
+   * a non-empty word composed of digits, letters, underscores and hyphens.
+   *
+   * @return The header code
+   */
+  String getHeader();
+
+  /* Name well-formedness checks */
+
+  /**
+   * Validate a user name.
+   *
+   * @param name The name to validate
+   */
+  static void isValidUserId(String name) {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L44" title="All 4 branches missed.">    if (name.isEmpty() || name.length() &gt; 8) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L45">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;User name should be non-empty and not longer than 8 characters.&quot;);
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L48" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (!name.matches(&quot;^[a-zA-Z0-9]*$&quot;)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L49">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;User name should be alphanumeric, not: &quot; + name);
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L52">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Validate a ticket tag name.
+   *
+   * @param name The name to validate
+   */
+  static void isValidTag(String name) {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L60" title="All 4 branches missed.">    if (name.isEmpty() || name.length() &gt; 8) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L61">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;Tag name should be non-empty and not longer than 8 characters.&quot;);
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L64" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (!name.matches(</span>
+        &quot;^[a-zA-Z0-9]*$&quot;)) {
+<span class="nc" id="L66">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;Toag should be alphanumeric, not: &quot; + name);
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L69">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Validate a tine msg line.
+   *
+   * @param msg The line to validate
+   */
+  static void isValidLine(String msg) {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L77" title="All 4 branches missed.">    if (msg.isEmpty() || msg.length() &gt; 48) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L78">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;Tine message line should be non-empty and not longer than 48&quot;
+          + &quot;characters.&quot;);
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L82" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (msg.contains(System.getProperty(&quot;line.separator&quot;))) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L83">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;Tine message line should be a single line, not: &quot; + msg);
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L86">  }</span>
+}

+ * append a list of tines from a user to each (possibly new) tag in the set
+ * of tags.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Instances of this class are immutable.

+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public final class Push implements Message {
+
+  /** 
+   * Pushing a Tine with this exact message line causes the server to close the
+   * ticket, if the user is the ticket's creator (initial author)
+   */
+  public static final String CLOSE_LINE = &quot;##CLOSE##&quot;;
+
+  private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;  // Generated

+  public final List&lt;String&gt; lines;

+   * singleton containing {@code tag}.

+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidTag(String)
+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidLine(String)
+   */
+  public Push(final String user, final String tag,
+      final List&lt;String&gt; lines) {

+import java.util.Collections;
+import java.util.Iterator;
+import java.util.List;
+import java.util.stream.Collectors;
+
+/**
+ * A {@code READ-REPLY} message: the server reply to a
+ * {@linkplain sep.tinee.net.message.ReadRequest READ} request: the list of
+ * lines recorded by the server for the specified tag, listed from the specified
+ * index.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Instances of this class are immutable.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public final class ReadReply implements Message {
+
+  private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;  // Default
+
+  /**
+   * The header code.
+   */
+  public static final String HEADER = &quot;READ-REPLY&quot;;
+
+  /**
+   * A list naming the users who authored the requested tines. The size of this
+   * list and the order of the items contained corresponds to that of {@link
+   * #lines}. It may be empty.
+   */
+  public final List&lt;String&gt; users;
+
+  /**
+   * A list of the message lines of the requested tines. The size of this list and
+   * the order of the items contained corresponds to that of {@link #users}. It
+   * may be empty.
+   */
+  public final List&lt;String&gt; lines;
+
+  /**
+   * Create a new {@code READ-REPLY} message. (Used by a server.)
+   *
+   * @param users The list of user names of the tine authors
+   * @param lines The list of requested tine message lines
+   * @throws IllegalArgumentException If users or lines is empty, or any of the
+   *                                  users names or message lines are invalid
+   *
+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidUserId(String)
+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidLine(String)
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L66">  public ReadReply(final List&lt;String&gt; users, final List&lt;String&gt; lines) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L67" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (users.size() != lines.size()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L68">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(</span>
+          &quot;users and lines must be the same size: &quot; + users + &quot; , &quot; + lines);
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L71">    users.forEach(Message::isValidUserId);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L72">    lines.forEach(Message::isValidLine);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L73">    this.users = Collections.unmodifiableList(users);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L74">    this.lines = Collections.unmodifiableList(lines);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L75">  }</span>
+

+  public String getHeader() {
+<span class="nc" id="L79">    return ReadReply.HEADER;</span>

+  }

+package sep.tinee.net.message;

+/**
+ * A {@code READ} message: tells a {@link sep.tinee.server.Server} instance to
+ return the currently recorded (sub)list of tines for a given tag, as
+ listed from the specified index (inclusive, starting from index 0).
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * After sending this message, the client should expected receive a
+ * {@link sep.tinee.net.message.ReadReply}.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Instances of this class are immutable.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public final class ReadRequest implements Message {
+
+  private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;  // Default
+
+  /**
+   * The header code.
+   */
+  public static final String HEADER = &quot;READ&quot;;
+
+  /**
+   * The specified tag.
+   */
+  public final String tag;
+
+  /**
+   * The specified index.
+   */
+  public final int index;  // Invariant: index &gt;= 0 (starts at 0)
+
+  /**
+   * Create a {@code READ} message with implicit index 0. This is equivalent to
+   * {@linkplain #ReadRequest(String, int)}{@code (tag, 0)}.
+   *
+   * @param tag The target tag
+   * @throws IllegalArgumentException If the tag is invalid or the index is
+                                  negative
+   *
+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidTag(String)
+   */
+  public ReadRequest(final String tag) {
+<span class="nc" id="L59">    this(tag, 0);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L60">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * Create a {@code READ} message. Note: it does not matter whether or not the
+ tag is explicitly recorded by the server.
+   *
+   * @param tag The target tag
+   * @param index The starting index (inclusive) of the list of tines to return
+   * @throws IllegalArgumentException If the tag is invalid or the index is
+                                  negative
+   *
+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidTag(String)
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L73">  public ReadRequest(final String tag, final int index) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L74">    Message.isValidTag(tag);</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L75" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (index &lt; 0) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L76">      throw new IllegalArgumentException(&quot;Invalid index value: &quot; + index);</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L78">    this.tag = tag;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L79">    this.index = index;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L80">  }</span>
+
+  @Override
+  public String getHeader() {
+<span class="nc" id="L84">    return ReadRequest.HEADER;</span>
+  }
+
+  @Override
+  public String toString() {
+<span class="nc" id="L89">    return ReadRequest.HEADER + &quot; &quot; + this.index + &quot; &quot; + this.tag;</span>

+  }

+/**
+ * A {@code SHOW-REPLY} message: the server reply to a
+ * {@linkplain sep.tinee.net.message.ShowRequest SHOW} request: the set of
+ * tags explicitly recorded by the server. The set may be empty.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public final class ShowReply implements Message {
+
+  private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;  // Default
+
+  /**
+   * The header code.
+   */
+  public static final String HEADER = &quot;SHOW-REPLY&quot;;
+
+  /**
+   * A set of the ticket tags explicitly recorded by the server. Possibly empty.
+   * Not modifiable.
+   */
+  public final Map&lt;String, String&gt; tags;
+
+  /**
+   * Create a new {@code SHOW-REPLY} message. (Used by a server.)
+   *
+   * @param tags The set of requested tags
+   * @throws IllegalArgumentException If any tag is invalid
+   *
+   * @see sep.tinee.net.message.Message#isValidTag(String)
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L53">  public ShowReply(final LinkedHashMap&lt;String, String&gt; tags) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L54" title="All 2 branches missed.">    for (Entry&lt;String, String&gt; e : tags.entrySet()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L55">      Message.isValidTag(e.getKey());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L56">      Message.isValidUserId(e.getValue());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L57">    }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L58">    this.tags = Collections.unmodifiableMap(new LinkedHashMap&lt;&gt;(tags));</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L59">  }</span>
+
+  @Override
+  public String getHeader() {
+<span class="nc" id="L63">    return ShowReply.HEADER;</span>
+  }
+
+  @Override
+  public String toString() {
+<span class="nc" id="L68">    return ShowReply.HEADER + &quot; &quot;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L69">        + this.tags.entrySet().stream()</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L70">            .map(x -&gt; &quot;(#&quot; + x.getKey() + &quot;, &quot; + x.getValue() + &quot;)&quot;)</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L71">            .collect(Collectors.joining(&quot; &quot;));</span>
+  }

+package sep.tinee.net.message;
+
+/**
+ * A {@code SHOW} message: tells a {@link sep.tinee.server.Server} instance
+ * to return the currently recorded set of ticket tags and creators (user
+ * names). This set may be empty.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * After sending this message, the client should expected receive a
+ * {@link sep.tinee.net.message.ShowReply}.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Instances of this class are immutable.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public final class ShowRequest implements Message {
+
+  private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;  // Default
+
+  /**
+   * The header code.
+   */
+  public static final String HEADER = &quot;SHOW&quot;;
+
+  /**
+   * Create a new {@code SHOW} message.
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L41">  public ShowRequest() {</span>
+    // Empty constructor
+<span class="nc" id="L43">  }</span>
+
+  @Override
+  public String getHeader() {
+<span class="nc" id="L47">    return ShowRequest.HEADER;</span>
+  }
+
+  @Override
+  public String toString() {
+<span class="nc" id="L52">    return ShowRequest.HEADER;</span>
+
+  }
+}

+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},

+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}. Finally, you submit only your client code, which
+ * will be tested against the base framework as provided.
+ *
+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.
+ */
+package sep.tinee.server;
+
+import java.util.Objects;
+
+/**
+ * Helper utility for {@link sep.tinee.server.Server} - namely, a tine is a
+ * pair of strings (username, line).
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * The references of a &lt;tt&gt;Pair&lt;/tt&gt; to its elements cannot be changed after it
+ * is created. A &lt;tt&gt;Pair&lt;/tt&gt; is thus immutable if its elements are immutable.
+ *
+ * @param &lt;L&gt; The type of the left element
+ * @param &lt;R&gt; The type of the right element
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public class Pair&lt;L, R&gt; {
+
+  /**
+   * The left element of this pair.
+   */
+  public final L left;
+
+  /**
+   * The right element of this pair.
+   */
+  public final R right;
+
+  /**
+   * Create a new pair.
+   *
+   * @param left  The left element of the pair
+   * @param right The right element of the pair
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L49">  public Pair(final L left, final R right) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L50">    this.left = left;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L51">    this.right = right;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L52">  }</span>
+
+  @Override
+  public String toString() {
+<span class="nc" id="L56">    return &quot;(&quot; + this.left + &quot;, &quot; + this.right + &quot;)&quot;;</span>
+  }
+
+  // NetBeans generated
+  @Override
+  public int hashCode() {
+<span class="nc" id="L62">    int hash = 3;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L63">    hash = 89 * hash + Objects.hashCode(this.left);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L64">    hash = 89 * hash + Objects.hashCode(this.right);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L65">    return hash;</span>
+  }
+
+  // NetBeans generated
+  @Override
+  public boolean equals(Object obj) {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L71" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this == obj) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L72">      return true;</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L74" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (obj == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L75">      return false;</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L77" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (getClass() != obj.getClass()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L78">      return false;</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L80">    final Pair&lt;?, ?&gt; other = (Pair&lt;?, ?&gt;) obj;</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L81" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (!Objects.equals(this.left, other.left)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L82">      return false;</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L84" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (!Objects.equals(this.right, other.right)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L85">      return false;</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L87">    return true;</span>
+  }
+}

+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Strict//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-strict.dtd"><html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" lang="en"><head><meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html;charset=UTF-8"/><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/report.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="shortcut icon" href="../.resources/report.gif" type="image/gif"/><title>Server.java</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/prettify.css" type="text/css"/><script type="text/javascript" src="../.resources/prettify.js"></script></head><body onload="window['PR_TAB_WIDTH']=4;prettyPrint()"><div class="breadcrumb" id="breadcrumb"><span class="info"><a href="../.sessions.html" class="el_session">Sessions</a></span><a href="../index.html" class="el_report">JaCoCoverage analysis of project &quot;18001953&quot; (powered by JaCoCo from EclEmma)</a> &gt; <a href="index.source.html" class="el_package">sep.tinee.server</a> &gt; <span class="el_source">Server.java</span></div><h1>Server.java</h1><pre class="source lang-java linenums">/*
+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}, {@link sep.tinee.server} and
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}. Finally, you submit only your client code, which
+ * will be tested against the base framework as provided.
+ *
+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.
+ */
+package sep.tinee.server;
+
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.net.ServerSocket;
+import java.net.Socket;
+import java.net.SocketException;
+import java.util.Arrays;
+import java.util.Collections;
+import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
+import java.util.LinkedList;
+import java.util.List;
+import java.util.Map.Entry;
+import java.util.Set;
+import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentLinkedQueue;
+import java.util.logging.Level;
+import java.util.logging.Logger;
+import java.util.stream.Collectors;
+import java.util.stream.Stream;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.Message;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.Push;
+
+/**
+ * {@code Server} is a minimal but adequately functional and robust Tinee
+ * server for you to develop and test your client against.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * The argument required to run the server corresponds to {@link #Server(int)}:
+ * the port number that the server should listen on.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * You can compile and run this server using &lt;b&gt;NetBeans&lt;/b&gt;; e.g., right-click
+ * this file in the NetBeans editor and select &quot;Run File&quot;.  Note, to provide
+ * the above argument, you should set up a &lt;b&gt;run configuration&lt;/b&gt; for this
+ * class: {@literal -&gt;} &quot;Set Project Configuration&quot; {@literal -&gt;} &quot;Customize...&quot;
+ * {@literal -&gt;} &quot;New...&quot; -- the &quot;Main Class&quot; is
+ * {@code sep.tinee.server.Server}, and write the port value (e.g.,
+ * {@code 8888}) in &quot;Arguments&quot;.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Assuming compilation using NetBeans (etc.), you can also run {@code Server}
+ * from the command line, e.g., on Windows, run:
+ * &lt;ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li style=&quot;list-style-type: none;&quot;&gt;
+ * {@code C:\...\tinee&gt; java -cp build\classes sep.tinee.server.Server 8888}
+ * &lt;/ul&gt;
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * &lt;i&gt;Note:&lt;/i&gt; On some platforms (e.g., Windows), you may be prompted
+ * with a security warning due to the server opening a network socket. You must
+ * grant this permission for the server to function properly.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * An instance of {@code Server} understands and communicates the messages in
+ * {@link sep.tinee.net.message}.
+ * &lt;ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt; {@link sep.tinee.net.message.Bye} - tells the {@code Server} to end
+ * this communication session with the client.
+ * &lt;li&gt; {@link sep.tinee.net.message.ShowRequest} - request the set of ticket
+ * tags and creators (user names) recorded by the {@code Server}.
+ * &lt;ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt; {@link sep.tinee.net.message.ShowReply} - the {@code Server}'s
+ * reply: the set of ticket tags and creators (possibly empty).
+ * &lt;/ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt; {@link sep.tinee.net.message.ReadRequest} - request the (sub)list of
+ * tines recorded by the {@code Server} for the specified tag, from the
+ * specified index (inclusive, starting from index 0). Note: The tag may not
+ * be &lt;i&gt;explicitly&lt;/i&gt; recorded by the {@code Server}.
+ * &lt;ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt; {@link sep.tinee.net.message.ReadReply} - the {@code Server}'s reply:
+ * the list of tines (possibly empty).
+ * &lt;/ul&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt; {@link sep.tinee.net.message.Push} - append a non-empty list of
+ * tines to each (possibly new) tag in the non-empty set of ticket tags.
+ * &lt;/ul&gt;
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * Your client should use {@link sep.tinee.net.channel.ClientChannel} top send
+ * and receive messages of the above types with a server: see the
+ * {@link sep.tinee.net.channel.ClientChannel#send(Message)} and
+ * {@link sep.tinee.net.channel.ClientChannel#receive()} methods.
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public class Server implements AutoCloseable {
+
+  protected final boolean debug;
+
+  private final ServerSocket servSock;
+
+<span class="nc" id="L98">  private final Object mutex = new Object();</span>
+
+<span class="nc" id="L100">  private final ConcurrentLinkedQueue&lt;Thread&gt; threads</span>
+      = new ConcurrentLinkedQueue&lt;&gt;();
+
+  /*
+   * {@code db} maps a tag to a list of (user, line) pairs.
+   * {@code Server} is neutral w.r.t. tag/line data types used by a client -
+   * it simply records tags, user names and text as strings.
+   * Invariant: Push.CLOSE_LINE only occurs in last pair of any tag.
+   * Invariant: a CLOSE_LINE user is the same as the first line user
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L110">  protected final LinkedHashMap&lt;String, List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt;&gt; db</span>
+      = new LinkedHashMap&lt;&gt;();
+
+  /**
+   * Create a new Tinee server bound to the specified port. This is
+   * equivalent to
+   * {@linkplain #Server(boolean,int) Server}{@code (false, port)}.
+   *
+   * @param port The port number that the server will listen on
+   * @throws IOException If the server socket could not be opened
+   */
+  
+  public Server(final int port) throws IOException {
+<span class="nc" id="L123">    this(false, port);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L124">  }</span>
+
+ 
+ 
+  /**
+   * Create a new Tinee server, bound to the specified port, with debug
+   * output enabled or disabled.
+   *
+   * @param debug Enable or disable local debug output printing ({@code true}
+   *              means enabled)
+   * @param port  The port number that the servSock will listen on
+   * @throws IOException If the server socket could not be opened
+   */
+<span class="nc" id="L137">  public Server(final boolean debug, final int port) throws IOException {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L138">    this.debug = debug;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L139">    this.servSock = new ServerSocket(port);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L140">  }</span>
+
+  /**
+   * To be called once, and once only, on a {@code Server} instance to start
+   * accepting and serving client connections.
+   */
+  public void run() {
+    while (true) {
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L149">        final Socket s = this.servSock.accept();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L150">        Thread t = new ServerThread(this, s);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L151">        this.threads.add(t);  // TODO: currently never cleaned</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L152">        t.start();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L153">      } catch (SocketException ex) {</span>
+        // Server socket closed -- swallow silently
+<span class="nc" id="L155">      } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L156">        Logger.getLogger(Server.class.getName()).log(Level.WARNING,</span>
+            &quot;Connection accept error: &quot;, ex);
+<span class="nc" id="L158">      }</span>
+    }
+  }
+
+  /**
+   * Shut down this Tinee server.
+   */
+  @Override
+  public void close() {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L167" title="All 2 branches missed.">    for (Thread t : this.threads) {</span>
+      try {
+<span class="nc" id="L169">        t.join(1000);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L170">      } catch (InterruptedException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L171">        throw new RuntimeException(ex);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L172">      }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L173">    }</span>
+    try {
+<span class="nc" id="L175">      this.servSock.close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L176">    } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L177">      Logger.getLogger(Server.class.getName()).log(Level.WARNING,</span>
+          &quot;Server socket close error: &quot;, ex);
+<span class="nc" id="L179">    }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L180">  }</span>
+
+  /* Tines -- synchronized routines (keep critical sections small) */
+
+  protected void addTines(final Set&lt;String&gt; tags,
+      List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; tines) {
+
+<span class="nc" id="L187">    synchronized (this.mutex) {</span>
+      //Date now = Calendar.getInstance().getTime();
+      //String stamp = new SimpleDateFormat(&quot;dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm&quot;).format(now);  // Inconvenient for testing
+      nextTag:
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L191" title="All 2 branches missed.">      for (final String tag : tags) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L192">        List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; curr = this.db.get(tag);</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L193" title="All 2 branches missed.">        if (curr == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L194">          curr = new LinkedList&lt;&gt;();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L195">          this.db.put(tag, curr);</span>
+        }
+
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L198" title="All 2 branches missed.">        boolean isClosed = !curr.isEmpty()</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L199" title="All 2 branches missed.">            &amp;&amp; curr.get(curr.size() - 1).right.equals(Push.CLOSE_LINE);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L200">        int i = 0;</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L201" title="All 2 branches missed.">        for (Pair&lt;String, String&gt; tine : tines) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L202" title="All 2 branches missed.">          if (isClosed) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L203">            String msg = &quot;Tag already closed, discarding: &quot;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L204">                + tines.subList(i, tines.size());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L205">            Logger.getLogger(Server.class.getName()).log(Level.WARNING, msg);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L206">            continue nextTag;</span>
+          }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L208" title="All 2 branches missed.">          if (tine.right.equals(Push.CLOSE_LINE)) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L209" title="All 4 branches missed.">            if (!curr.isEmpty() &amp;&amp; !tine.left.equals(curr.get(0).left)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L210">              String msg = &quot;Discarding invalid close by &quot; + tine.left</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L211">                  + &quot;, tag owned by &quot; + curr.get(0).left;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L212">              Logger.getLogger(Server.class.getName()).log(Level.WARNING, msg);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L213">            } else {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L214">              isClosed = true;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L215">              curr.add(tine);</span>
+            }
+          } else {
+<span class="nc" id="L218">            curr.add(tine);</span>
+          }
+<span class="nc" id="L220">          i++;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L221">        }</span>
+
+<span class="nc" id="L223">      }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L224">    }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L225">  }</span>
+
+  // @return map: tag -&gt; creator  -- keyset ordered following this.db
+  protected LinkedHashMap&lt;String, String&gt; getTags() {
+<span class="nc" id="L229">    synchronized (this.mutex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L230">      return this.db.entrySet().stream().collect(</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L231">          Collectors.toMap(Entry::getKey, e -&gt; e.getValue().get(0).left,</span>
+              (x, y) -&gt; {
+<span class="nc" id="L233">                throw new RuntimeException(&quot;Tags not distinct?&quot;);</span>
+              }, LinkedHashMap::new));
+<span class="nc" id="L235">    }</span>
+  }
+
+  // Pre: index &gt;= 0 -- guaranteed by ReadRequest
+  protected List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; getTines(final String tag,
+      final int index) {
+<span class="nc" id="L241">    synchronized (this.mutex) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L242" title="All 2 branches missed.">      if (!this.db.containsKey(tag)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L243">        return Collections.emptyList();</span>
+      }
+<span class="nc" id="L245">      final List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; tines = this.db.get(tag);</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L246" title="All 2 branches missed.">      if (index &gt;= tines.size()) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L247">        return Collections.emptyList();</span>
+      }
+<span class="nc" id="L249">      return Collections.unmodifiableList(tines.subList(index, tines.size()));</span>
+      // ^Because SubList is not Seriablizable
+<span class="nc" id="L251">    }</span>
+  }
+
+  /* Main */
+
+  /**
+   * Create and run a {@code Server} instance.
+   *
+   * @param args Use {@code -h} to list the supported options
+   * @throws IOException If the servSock could not be created
+   */
+  public static void main(final String[] args) throws IOException {
+<span class="nc" id="L263">    final String help</span>
+        = &quot;Usage:  java [-cp ...] sep.tinee.server.Server [-s] port\n&quot;
+        + &quot;            --silent -s  Suppress debug messages\n&quot;
+        + &quot;            --help   -h  Print this help message&quot;;
+<span class="nc" id="L267">    if (Arrays.stream(args)</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L268" title="All 6 branches missed.">        .anyMatch(x -&gt; &quot;--help&quot;.equals(x) || &quot;-h&quot;.equals(x))) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L269">      System.out.println(help);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L270">      System.exit(0);</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L271" title="All 2 branches missed.">    } else if (args.length &lt; 1) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L272">      System.err.println(help);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L273">      System.exit(1);</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L275">    final int port = Integer.parseInt(args[args.length - 1]);</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L276" title="All 2 branches missed.">    final boolean silent = args.length &gt; 1</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L277" title="All 2 branches missed.">        &amp;&amp; Stream.of(&quot;--silent&quot;, &quot;-s&quot;).anyMatch(x -&gt; x.equals(args[0]));</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L278" title="All 2 branches missed.">    try (final Server s = new Server(!silent, port)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L279">      s.run();</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L280" title="All 8 branches missed.">    }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L281">  }</span>
+}

+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Strict//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-strict.dtd"><html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" lang="en"><head><meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html;charset=UTF-8"/><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/report.css" type="text/css"/><link rel="shortcut icon" href="../.resources/report.gif" type="image/gif"/><title>ServerThread.java</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="../.resources/prettify.css" type="text/css"/><script type="text/javascript" src="../.resources/prettify.js"></script></head><body onload="window['PR_TAB_WIDTH']=4;prettyPrint()"><div class="breadcrumb" id="breadcrumb"><span class="info"><a href="../.sessions.html" class="el_session">Sessions</a></span><a href="../index.html" class="el_report">JaCoCoverage analysis of project &quot;18001953&quot; (powered by JaCoCo from EclEmma)</a> &gt; <a href="index.source.html" class="el_package">sep.tinee.server</a> &gt; <span class="el_source">ServerThread.java</span></div><h1>ServerThread.java</h1><pre class="source lang-java linenums">/*
+ * This file is part of the base framework for the 6COM1038 Software Engineering
+ * Practice coursework assessments -- a command line client application for a
+ * text-based Ticket System.
+ *
+ * &lt;i&gt;Warning:&lt;/i&gt; you are advised &lt;b&gt;not&lt;/b&gt; to modify this file, nor any of
+ * the base framework, i.e., the packages {@link sep.tinee.server},
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}, {@link sep.tinee.server} and
+ * {@link sep.tinee.server}. Finally, you submit only your client code, which
+ * will be tested against the base framework as provided.
+ *
+ * If you do wish to (temporarily) modify the base framework for debugging or
+ * your own interest, please bear in mind the above point.
+ */
+package sep.tinee.server;
+
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.io.ObjectInputStream;
+import java.io.ObjectOutputStream;
+import java.net.Socket;
+import java.util.List;
+import java.util.logging.Level;
+import java.util.logging.Logger;
+import java.util.stream.Collectors;
+import java.util.stream.Stream;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.Bye;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.Message;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.ShowReply;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.ReadRequest;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.ReadReply;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.Push;
+import sep.tinee.net.message.ShowRequest;
+
+/**
+ * To be spawned by {@link sep.tinee.server.Server} to serve one Tinee
+ * client (concurrently with any other clients in other server threads).
+ *
+ * @author rhu1 {@literal &lt;r.z.h.hu@herts.ac.uk&gt;}
+ */
+public class ServerThread extends Thread {
+
+  private final Server server;
+  private final Socket sock;
+  private final ObjectInputStream in;
+  private final ObjectOutputStream out;
+
+  /**
+   * Create a thread object for serving the connected Tinee client.
+   *
+   * @param server The {@link sep.tinee.server.Server} that is spawning this
+   *               thread
+   * @param sock   The server-side {@link java.net.Socket} of the channel
+   *               established with the client
+   * @throws IOException If I/O streams cannot be established with the client
+   *                     over the socket.
+   */
+  public ServerThread(final Server server, final Socket sock) throws
+<span class="nc" id="L58">      IOException {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L59">    this.server = server;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L60">    this.sock = sock;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L61">    this.in = new ObjectInputStream(sock.getInputStream());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L62">    this.out = new ObjectOutputStream(sock.getOutputStream());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L63">  }</span>
+
+  @Override
+  public void run() {
+<span class="nc" id="L67">    debugPrintln(&quot;Accepted connection.&quot;);</span>
+    try {
+      while (true) {
+<span class="nc" id="L70">        Object read = this.in.readObject();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L71">        debugPrintln(&quot;Received: &quot; + read);</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L72" title="All 2 branches missed.">        if (!(read instanceof Message)) {  // Could replace by a separate header communication</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L73">          throw new IOException(getFormattedClientAddr()</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L74">              + &quot;Client error, invalid message: &quot; + read.getClass());</span>
+        }
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L76" title="All 2 branches missed.">        if (handleMessage((Message) read)) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L77">          return;</span>
+        }
+<span class="nc" id="L79">      }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L80">    } catch (IOException | ClassNotFoundException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L81">      final String msg = getFormattedClientAddr() + &quot; I/O error: &quot;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L82">          + ex.getMessage() + &quot; (&quot; + ex.getClass().getSimpleName() + &quot;)&quot;;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L83">      Logger.getLogger(ServerThread.class.getName()).log(Level.SEVERE, msg, ex);</span>
+    } finally {
+<span class="nc" id="L85">      close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L86">      debugPrintln(&quot;Session ended.&quot;);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L87">    }</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L88">  }</span>
+
+  // @return  is terminal
+  private boolean handleMessage(final Message msg) throws IOException {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L92" title="All 18 branches missed.">    switch (msg.getHeader()) {</span>
+      case Bye.HEADER:
+<span class="nc" id="L94">        return true;  // close done by calling method (run) finally</span>
+      case ShowRequest.HEADER: {
+<span class="nc" id="L96">        final Message rep = new ShowReply(this.server.getTags());  // Non-empty</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L97">        this.out.reset();  // O/w seems to cache the List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; instance reused throughout</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L98">        this.out.writeObject(rep);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L99">        this.out.flush();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L100">        debugPrintln(&quot;Sent: &quot; + rep);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L101">        break;</span>
+      }
+      case ReadRequest.HEADER: {
+<span class="nc" id="L104">        final ReadRequest req = (ReadRequest) msg;  // pub.index &gt;= 0</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L105">        final List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; tines</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L106">            = this.server.getTines(req.tag, req.index);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L107">        final Pair&lt;Stream&lt;String&gt;, Stream&lt;String&gt;&gt; reduce</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L108">            = tines.stream().map(x -&gt; new Pair&lt;&gt;(</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L109">            Stream.of(x.left), Stream.of(x.right)))</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L110">                .reduce(new Pair&lt;&gt;(Stream.empty(), Stream.empty()),</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L111">                    (z, y) -&gt; new Pair&lt;&gt;(</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L112">                        Stream.concat(z.left, y.left),</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L113">                        Stream.concat(z.right, y.right)));</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L114">        final Pair&lt;List&lt;String&gt;, List&lt;String&gt;&gt; pair</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L115">            = new Pair&lt;&gt;(reduce.left.collect(Collectors.toList()),</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L116">                reduce.right.collect(Collectors.toList()));</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L117">        final Message rep = new ReadReply(pair.left, pair.right);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L118">        this.out.reset();  // O/w seems to cache the List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; instance reused throughout</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L119">        this.out.writeObject(rep);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L120">        this.out.flush();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L121">        debugPrintln(&quot;Sent: &quot; + rep);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L122">        break;</span>
+      }
+      case Push.HEADER: {
+<span class="nc" id="L125">        final Push pub = (Push) msg;</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L126">        Message.isValidUserId(pub.user);  // Only needed if Message further subclassed</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L127">        pub.tags.forEach(Message::isValidTag);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L128">        pub.lines.stream().forEach(Message::isValidLine);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L129">        final List&lt;Pair&lt;String, String&gt;&gt; tines</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L130">            = pub.lines.stream().map(x -&gt; new Pair&lt;&gt;(pub.user, x))</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L131">                .collect(Collectors.toList());</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L132">        this.server.addTines(pub.tags, tines);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L133">        break;</span>
+      }
+      default:
+<span class="nc" id="L136">        throw new IOException(getFormattedClientAddr()</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L137">            + &quot;Client error, unexpected message: &quot; + msg.getClass());</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L139">    return false;</span>
+  }
+
+  private void close() {
+<span class="nc" id="L143">    debugPrintln(&quot;Closing connection.&quot;);</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L144">    IOException err = null;</span>
+    try {
+<span class="nc" id="L146">      this.in.close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L147">    } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L148">      err = ex;  // msg currently null</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L149">    }</span>
+    try {
+<span class="nc" id="L151">      this.out.close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L152">    } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L153" title="All 2 branches missed.">      if (err == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L154">        err = ex;</span>
+      }
+<span class="nc" id="L156">    }</span>
+    try {
+<span class="nc" id="L158">      this.sock.close();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L159">    } catch (IOException ex) {</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L160" title="All 2 branches missed.">      if (err == null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L161">        err = ex;</span>
+      }
+<span class="nc" id="L163">    }</span>
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L164" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (err != null) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L165">      final String msg = &quot;Connection close error: &quot; + err.getMessage();</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L166">      Logger.getLogger(ServerThread.class.getName()).log(Level.SEVERE, msg);</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L168">  }</span>
+
+  private void debugPrintln(final String msg) {
+<span class="nc bnc" id="L171" title="All 2 branches missed.">    if (this.server.debug) {</span>
+<span class="nc" id="L172">      System.out.println(getFormattedClientAddr() + &quot; &quot; + msg);</span>
+    }
+<span class="nc" id="L174">  }</span>
+
+  private String getFormattedClientAddr() {
+<span class="nc" id="L177">    return &quot;(Client &quot; + sock.getRemoteSocketAddress() + &quot;)&quot;;</span>
+  }
+
+}
+</pre><div class="footer"><span class="right">Created with <a href="http://www.eclemma.org/jacoco">JaCoCo</a> 0.7.6.201602180812</span></div></body></html>

+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
+<!-- You may freely edit this file. See commented blocks below for -->
+<!-- some examples of how to customize the build. -->
+<!-- (If you delete it and reopen the project it will be recreated.) -->
+<!-- By default, only the Clean and Build commands use this build script. -->
+<!-- Commands such as Run, Debug, and Test only use this build script if -->
+<!-- the Compile on Save feature is turned off for the project. -->
+<!-- You can turn off the Compile on Save (or Deploy on Save) setting -->
+<!-- in the project's Project Properties dialog box.-->
+<project name="18001953" default="default" basedir=".">
+    <description>Builds, tests, and runs the project 18001953.</description>
+    <import file="nbproject/build-impl.xml"/>
+    <!--
+
+    There exist several targets which are by default empty and which can be 
+    used for execution of your tasks. These targets are usually executed 
+    before and after some main targets. They are: 
+
+      -pre-init:                 called before initialization of project properties
+      -post-init:                called after initialization of project properties
+      -pre-compile:              called before javac compilation
+      -post-compile:             called after javac compilation
+      -pre-compile-single:       called before javac compilation of single file
+      -post-compile-single:      called after javac compilation of single file
+      -pre-compile-test:         called before javac compilation of JUnit tests
+      -post-compile-test:        called after javac compilation of JUnit tests
+      -pre-compile-test-single:  called before javac compilation of single JUnit test
+      -post-compile-test-single: called after javac compilation of single JUunit test
+      -pre-jar:                  called before JAR building
+      -post-jar:                 called after JAR building
+      -post-clean:               called after cleaning build products
+
+    (Targets beginning with '-' are not intended to be called on their own.)
+
+    Example of inserting an obfuscator after compilation could look like this:
+
+        <target name="-post-compile">
+            <obfuscate>
+                <fileset dir="${build.classes.dir}"/>
+            </obfuscate>
+        </target>
+
+    For list of available properties check the imported 
+    nbproject/build-impl.xml file. 
+
+
+    Another way to customize the build is by overriding existing main targets.
+    The targets of interest are: 
+
+      -init-macrodef-javac:     defines macro for javac compilation
+      -init-macrodef-junit:     defines macro for junit execution
+      -init-macrodef-debug:     defines macro for class debugging
+      -init-macrodef-java:      defines macro for class execution
+      -do-jar:                  JAR building
+      run:                      execution of project 
+      -javadoc-build:           Javadoc generation
+      test-report:              JUnit report generation
+
+    An example of overriding the target for project execution could look like this:
+
+        <target name="run" depends="18001953-impl.jar">
+            <exec dir="bin" executable="launcher.exe">
+                <arg file="${dist.jar}"/>
+            </exec>
+        </target>
+
+    Notice that the overridden target depends on the jar target and not only on 
+    the compile target as the regular run target does. Again, for a list of available 
+    properties which you can use, check the target you are overriding in the
+    nbproject/build-impl.xml file. 
+
+    -->
+</project>

+========================
+BUILD OUTPUT DESCRIPTION
+========================
+
+When you build an Java application project that has a main class, the IDE
+automatically copies all of the JAR
+files on the projects classpath to your projects dist/lib folder. The IDE
+also adds each of the JAR files to the Class-Path element in the application
+JAR files manifest file (MANIFEST.MF).
+
+To run the project from the command line, go to the dist folder and
+type the following:
+
+java -jar "18001953.jar" 
+
+To distribute this project, zip up the dist folder (including the lib folder)
+and distribute the ZIP file.
+
+Notes:
+
+* If two JAR files on the project classpath have the same name, only the first
+JAR file is copied to the lib folder.
+* Only JAR files are copied to the lib folder.
+If the classpath contains other types of files or folders, these files (folders)
+are not copied.
+* If a library on the projects classpath also has a Class-Path element
+specified in the manifest,the content of the Class-Path element has to be on
+the projects runtime path.
+* To set a main class in a standard Java project, right-click the project node
+in the Projects window and choose Properties. Then click Run and enter the
+class name in the Main Class field. Alternatively, you can manually type the
+class name in the manifest Main-Class element.
